###### SETUP ######

gaudi.1 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

    hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_variable = gaudi_magnetic_association_member_var
	}

	###############################################################################
	# PHYSICS                                                                	  #
	###############################################################################
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_verrier_observatory
					has_active_production_method = pm_gaudi_magnetic_observatory
				}
			}
			gaudi_add_x_magnetic_data = {
				AMOUNT = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###### ART NOUVEAU & ART DECO ######

#Gaudí 21: Art Nouveau city quarter

gaudi.21 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

    title = gaudi.21.t
		
    desc = gaudi.21.d

	flavor = gaudi.21.f

	duration = 3
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/elgar_pictures/elgar_art_nouveau.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_music.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = gaudi_art_nouveau_quarter_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_art_nouveau_quarter_state
		}
	}

	option = { #We are a leading cultural nation
		name = gaudi.21.g
		gaudi_add_1_splendid_architecture = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_journal_entry = {
        		type = je_gaudi_art_nouveau_quarter 
			}
        }
	}
}

###### SUMMER PALACE ######

#Gaudí 60: Burning the Summer Palace

gaudi.60 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

    title = gaudi.60.t
		
    desc = gaudi.60.d

	flavor = gaudi.60.f

	duration = 3

	placement = scope:gaudi_summer_palace_state
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_summer_burning.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_military.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BEIJING
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_summer_palace_state
		}
	}

	option = { #Burn it down!
		name = gaudi.60.g
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = gaudi.60.tt
		add_treasury = 100000
		lepsius_add_5_fareastern_artifact = yes
		lepsius_add_1_major_fareastern_artifact = yes
		change_infamy = 10
		set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_summer_found_var
		#This is used to keep track of the country and year of the discovery of the Artifact
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_variable = lepsius_summer_discoverer_global_var
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_summer_discoverer_global_var
				value = root.country_definition
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_summer_year_global_var
				value = year
			}
		}
		set_global_variable = gaudi_summer_palace_looted
		c:CHI = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -25
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = gaudi.61
				popup = yes
			}
		}
		post_notification = gaudi_summer_palace_burned_notification
	}

	option = { #Only barbarians would think of that.
		name = gaudi.60.h
		change_infamy = -2

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 61: The Destruction of the Summer Palace

gaudi.61 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

    title = gaudi.61.t
		
    desc = gaudi.61.d

	flavor = gaudi.60.f

	duration = 3
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_summer_burning.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BEIJING
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_summer_palace_state
		}
	}

	option = { #We are truly going through a valley of tears ...
		name = gaudi.61.g
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_national_monument_burned_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:gaudi_summer_palace_state = {
			remove_building = "building_gaudi_summer"
		}
	}
}

		change_infamy = 3
		c:GBR = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -25
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = gaudi.63
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Only barbarians would think of that.
		name = gaudi.60.h
		change_infamy = -2

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

######COLLAPS OF THE CAMPANILE######

#Gaudí 70: The Campanile has collapsed!

gaudi.70 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

    title = gaudi.70.t
		
    desc = gaudi.70.d

	flavor = gaudi.70.f

	duration = 3
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_campanile_collapsed.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"

	trigger = {
		game_date >= 1902.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = gaudi_campanile_collapsed_var
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_VENETIA
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_VENETIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_campanile_state
		}
		set_global_variable = gaudi_campanile_collapsed_var
	}

	option = { #We are truly going through a valley of tears ...
		name = gaudi.70.g
		default_option = yes
		add_treasury = -50000
		set_variable = {
			name = gaudi_campanile_progress
			value = 0
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
        	type = je_gaudi_rebuild_campanile
        }
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_campanile_cost_modifier
		}
		scope:gaudi_campanile_state = {
			deactivate_building = {
				building = "building_gaudi_campanile"
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Build something new!
		name = gaudi.70.h
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = elgar_art_nouveau_tech
		}
		add_treasury = -100000
		gaudi_add_1_splendid_architecture = yes
		scope:gaudi_campanile_state = {
			remove_building = "building_gaudi_campanile"
		}
	}

	option = { #We can't afford that.
		name = gaudi.70.i
		scope:gaudi_campanile_state = {
			remove_building = "building_gaudi_campanile"
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = 0.2
				culture = cu:north_italian
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_no_campanile_modifier
			years = 10
		}
	}
}

	hidden = yes

	}

	immediate = {
		change_variable = {
			name = gaudi_campanile_progress
			add = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = gaudi_engineer_var
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = gaudi_campanile_progress
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 80: Walhalla

gaudi.80 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.80.t
	desc = gaudi.80.d
	flavor = gaudi.80.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_walhalla.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"

	cooldown = {
		years = 100
	}

	trigger = {
		game_date >= 1840.1.1
		game_date <= 1850.1.1
		exists = c:BAV
		ROOT = c:BAV
		has_technology_researched = nationalism
		has_technology_researched = romanticism
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_BAVARIA
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = academics_ruler_scope
		}
	}

	option = { #Honor a German composer.
	default_option = yes
		name = gaudi.80.g
		elgar_add_x_music_tradition_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 10
		}
		elgar_small_add_technology = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
		}
	}

	option = { #Honor a German literary.
		name = gaudi.80.h
		manzoni_add_x_literary_tradition_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 10
		}
		elgar_small_add_technology = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
		}
	}

	option = { #Honor a German painter.
		name = gaudi.80.i
		klimt_add_x_painting_tradition_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 10
		}
		elgar_small_add_technology = yes
	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 90: Mysterious Whale sinks ship!

gaudi.90 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

    title = gaudi.90.t
		
    desc = gaudi.90.d

	flavor = gaudi.90.f

	duration = 3
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_nemo.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_navigation.dds"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_game_rule = lepsius_only_historical_rule
		}
		is_player = yes
		game_date >= 1869.1.1
		game_date < 1879.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = gaudi_nautilus_var
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			has_building = building_whaling_station
		}
		country_rank > rank_value:major_power
		has_global_variable = american_civil_war
		any_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_SINAI
			has_building = building_suez_canal
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = gaudi_nautilus_var
	}

	option = { #But is it really a whale?
		name = gaudi.90.g
		default_option = yes
		add_treasury = -10000
		add_journal_entry = {
        	type = je_gaudi_nemo
        }
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_nautilus_modifier
		}
	}
}

gaudi.95 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

    title = gaudi.95.t
		
    desc = gaudi.95.d

	flavor = gaudi.95.f

	duration = 3
		
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:dubois_naturalist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_navigation.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
		create_character = {
			dna = mr_pol_mieroslawski_adam
			first_name = gaudi_captain
			last_name = gaudi_nemo
			birth_date = 1808.2.24
			culture = cu:polish
			interest_group = ig_armed_forces
			female = no
			traits = { 
				wrathful
				brave
				innovative
				expert_naval_commander
			}
			is_admiral = yes
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 120
			}
	
			save_scope_as = gaudi_nemo_scope
		}
	}

	option = { #But is Captain Nemo really defeated?
		name = gaudi.95.g
		default_option = yes
		remove_modifier = gaudi_nautilus_modifier
		scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
		naturalist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "50"
		}
		dubois_large_add_technology = yes
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 5000 }
	}

	after = {
		scope:gaudi_nemo_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = no
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 116: Political Controversy

gaudi.116 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.116.t
	desc = gaudi.116.d
	flavor = gaudi.116.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_dom_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:union_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ig:ig_trade_unions = {
			is_in_government = no
			is_marginal = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_dombau_trade_ig_cooldown
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_NORTH_RHINE
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_dom_state
		}
		ig:ig_trade_unions = {
			save_scope_as = trade_unions_ig 
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = union_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.116.g #And the weather report?
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_1_dombau_progress = yes
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.116.h #He has a point
		gaudi_sub_6_dombau_progress = yes
		add_treasury = -10000
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		set_variable = {
			name = gaudi_dombau_trade_ig_cooldown
			days = 1000
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 118: A national or a religious Project? (Intelligentsia vs. devout)

gaudi.118 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.118.t
	desc = gaudi.118.d
	flavor = gaudi.118.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_dom_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:devout_leader
	right_icon = scope:intelligentsia_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_dombau_religion_nationalism_conflict_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = gaudi_dombau_religion_nationalism_conflict_var
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_NORTH_RHINE
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_dom_state
		}
		ig:ig_devout = {
			save_scope_as = devout_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = devout_leader
			}
		}
		ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
			save_scope_as = intelligentsia_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = intelligentsia_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.118.g #This is a national project
        gaudi_add_3_dombau_progress = yes
		scope:intelligentsia_ig  = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
		scope:devout_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.118.h #This is a national and a religious project
		gaudi_add_1_dombau_progress = yes
		default_option = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.118.i #This is a religious project
        gaudi_add_3_dombau_progress = yes
		scope:intelligentsia_ig  = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
		scope:devout_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

			has_variable = gaudi_romantic_ruler_support

		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = romantic
					has_trait = pious
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ruler
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.120.g #Our good [title] [fullname]!
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_6_dombau_progress = yes
		set_variable = {
			name = gaudi_romantic_ruler_support
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 121: Inviting an Ally

gaudi.121 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.121.t
	desc = gaudi.121.d
	flavor = gaudi.121.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_dom_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_dombau_section.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		any_country = {
			has_diplomatic_pact = {
				who = root
     			type = alliance 
     		}
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = gaudi_dombau_patron_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_NORTH_RHINE
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_dom_state
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = root
     				type = alliance 
     			}
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ally_nation
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.121.g #Invite our ally to visit Cologne.
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_3_dombau_progress = yes
		scope:gaudi_ally_nation = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 5
			}
		}
		scope:gaudi_ally_nation = {
			trigger_event = { 
				id = gaudi.122
				popup = yes 
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gaudi.121.h #This will only disturb our efforts.
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_1_dombau_progress = yes
	}
}

		name = gaudi.122.g #This splendid project should have our support.
        default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_dombau_patron_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			days = 1000
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_diplomatic_prestige_modifier
			days = 1000
		}
		scope:gaudi_dombau_nation = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 5
			}
		}
		scope:gaudi_dombau_nation = {
			trigger_event = { 
				id = gaudi.123
				popup = yes 
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gaudi.122.h #It's not that great after all.
		scope:gaudi_dombau_nation = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -5
			}
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 127: Archaeological investigations

gaudi.127 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.127.t
	desc = gaudi.127.d
	flavor = gaudi.127.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_dom_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_archaeologist

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_excavation_cologne
		}
		lepsius_has_active_archaeologist = yes
		global_var:gaudi_dombau_progress >= 12
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_NORTH_RHINE
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_dom_state
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = gaudi_archaeologist
		}
		set_variable = gaudi_excavation_cologne
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.127.g #We cannot afford such a long halt to construction.
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_1_dombau_progress = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.127.h #A unique archaeological opportunity.
		gaudi_sub_12_dombau_progress = yes
		lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = { 
			AMOUNT = 2 
		}
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "10"
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Gaudí 200: Alfred Escher [1849]

gaudi.200 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.200.t
	desc = gaudi.200.d
	flavor = gaudi.200.f

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_gotthard_escher.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		exists = c:SWI 
		ROOT = c:SWI #only for Switzerland
		NOT = { 
			has_variable = gaudi_alfred_escher_var
		}
		game_date >= 1849.1.1
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = gaudi_alfred_escher_var
	}

	option = { #He will serve us well
		name = gaudi.200.g
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_influence_of_escher_modifier
		}
		create_character = {
			first_name = gaudi_alfred
	  		last_name = gaudi_escher
	   		culture = cu:alemannic
    		female = no
    		religion = rel:protestant
    		ideology = ideology:ideology_market_liberal
			ig_leader = yes
    		interest_group = ig_industrialists
			dna = mr_swi_escher_alfred
    		birth_date = 1819.2.20
			historical = yes
    		traits = { 
				meticulous
				innovative
				ambitious
				arrogant
			}
			on_created = {
				set_variable = gaudi_is_alfred_escher_var
				set_variable = memento_mori_immunity
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #This man is too dangerous
		name = gaudi.200.h

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 202: Death of Alfred Escher [1882]

	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.202.t
	desc = gaudi.202.d
	flavor = gaudi.202.f

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_gotthard_escher.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		any_scope_character = {
			has_variable = gaudi_is_alfred_escher_var
		}
		NOT = { 
			has_variable = gaudi_alfred_escher_dead_var
		}
		game_date >= 1882.1.1
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = gaudi_alfred_escher_dead_var
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = gaudi_is_alfred_escher_var
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_alfred_escher
		}
	}

	option = { #He should enter politics
		name = gaudi.202.g
		scope:gaudi_alfred_escher = {
			kill_character = yes
		}
	}
}

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		mr_set_gotthard_state_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.213.g
        default_option = yes
        scope:gaudi_gotthard_state = {
        	add_modifier = {
        		name = gaudi_gotthard_construction_modifier
        	}
        }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_gotthard_construction_cost_modifier
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_player = no
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_gotthard_construction_cost_ai_modifier
			}
		}
        add_journal_entry = {
        	type = je_gaudi_gotthard_construction
        }
		add_journal_entry = {
        	type = je_gaudi_gotthard_discontent
        }
	}
}

	flavor = gaudi.214.f

	duration = 3

	}

	immediate = {
		mr_set_gotthard_state_effect = yes
		scope:gaudi_gotthard_state = {
			remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_bad_air_modifier
			remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_worker_influx_modifier
		}
		set_global_variable = gaudi_gotthard_construction_finished
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_italy_credit_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_germany_credit_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_bahngesellschaft_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_waterproofing_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_bonus_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_cutthroat_shops_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_cutthroat_shops_closed_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_clean_houses_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthart_better_conditions_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthart_best_conditions_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_foreign_investor_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_experts_modifier
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_worker_condition_worse_modifier
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.214.g
        default_option = yes
		remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_construction_cost_modifier
		scope:gaudi_gotthard_state = {
			remove_modifier = gaudi_gotthard_construction_modifier
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_gotthard_railway_modifier
			}
			create_building = {
 				building = "building_gaudi_gotthard"
				level = 1
 			}
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 240: Trade unions criticize Gotthard project

gaudi.240 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.240.t
	desc = gaudi.240.d
	flavor = gaudi.240.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_gotthard_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:union_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		global_var:gaudi_gotthard_discontent >= 5
		NOT = {
			has_modifier = gaudi_gotthart_better_conditions_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		mr_set_gotthard_state_effect = yes
		ig:ig_trade_unions = {
			save_scope_as = trade_unions_ig 
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = union_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.240.g #Doesn't this man understand the importance of our project?
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_1_gotthard_progress = yes
		gaudi_add_1_gotthard_discontent = yes
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.240.h #He has a point
		gaudi_sub_6_gotthard_progress = yes
		gaudi_sub_3_gotthard_discontent = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_gotthart_better_conditions_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 244: Magnificient explosions

gaudi.244 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.244.t
	desc = gaudi.244.d
	flavor = gaudi.244.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_gotthard_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_gotthard_tunnel.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_gotthard_explosions_var
		}
		any_scope_building = {
			is_building_type = building_chemical_plants
			OR = {
				has_active_production_method = pm_ammonia-soda_process
				has_active_production_method = pm_vacuum_evaporation
				has_active_production_method = pm_brine_electrolysis
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = gaudi_gotthard_explosions_var
		mr_set_gotthard_state_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_chemical_plants
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_explosives_state
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = gaudi.244.g #But that's checked for safety, isn't it?
		gaudi_add_12_gotthard_progress = yes
		scope:gaudi_explosives_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_gotthard_production_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_gotthard_break.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		global_var:gaudi_gotthard_discontent >= 5
		NOT = {
			has_modifier = gaudi_gotthart_better_conditions_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		mr_set_gotthard_state_effect = yes
		ig:ig_trade_unions = {
			save_scope_as = trade_unions_ig 
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = union_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.247.g #Call the vigilante.
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_sub_6_gotthard_progress = yes
		change_infamy = 1
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			65 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = gaudi.248
					popup = yes 
				}
			}
			35 = {
				hidden_effect = {
					add_journal_entry = {
        				type = je_gaudi_gotthard_discontent
        			}
					set_global_variable = {
						name = gaudi_gotthard_discontent
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.247.h #We give in to their demands.
		gaudi_sub_12_gotthard_progress = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_gotthart_best_conditions_modifier
			years = 8
		}
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_journal_entry = {
        		type = je_gaudi_gotthard_discontent
        	}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = gaudi_gotthard_discontent
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.318.t
	desc = gaudi.318.d
	flavor = gaudi.318.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_cristo_state

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	duration = 3

			has_modifier = gaudi_cristo_lightning_rod_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_RIO_DE_JANEIRO
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_cristo_state
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {

					has_war_with = ROOT

		}
	}

		default_option = yes
		scope:gaudi_cristo_neighbour = {

				country = ROOT
				value = 10
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = gaudi.318.h #
		gaudi_add_3_cristo_progress = yes
		add_treasury = 5000
	}

#Gaudí 319: Atheistic intervention

gaudi.319 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.319.t
	desc = gaudi.319.d
	flavor = gaudi.319.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_cristo_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_cristo_atheist

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		any_scope_character = {
			has_ideology = ideology:ideology_atheist
			NOT = {
				has_variable = gaudi_cristo_atheist
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_RIO_DE_JANEIRO
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_cristo_state
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_ideology = ideology:ideology_atheist
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_cristo_atheist
			set_variable = gaudi_cristo_atheist
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = gaudi.319.g #
		gaudi_sub_6_cristo_progress = yes
		default_option = yes
	}
	option = { 
		name = gaudi.319.h #
		gaudi_add_3_cristo_progress = yes
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				has_ideology = ideology:ideology_anti_clerical
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_christo_ig_rebuked_modifier
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = gaudi.319.i #
		gaudi_add_1_cristo_progress = yes
		scope:gaudi_cristo_atheist = {
			kill_character = yes 
		}
	}
}

			AMOUNT = 2

			AMOUNT = "10"
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

gaudi.423 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.423.t
	desc = gaudi.423.d
	flavor = gaudi.423.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_mole_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_nietzsche.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		game_date >= 1879.1.1
		NOT = {
			game_date >= 1889.1.3
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_nietzsche
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_PIEDMONT
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_mole_state
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.423.g #The man has taste. Not just since 'Morgenröte'.
        default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_nietzsche_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		set_variable = gaudi_nietzsche
	}
}

	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.424.t
	desc = gaudi.424.d
	flavor = gaudi.424.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_mole_state

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_mole_dome.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = curtiss_reconnaissance_balloon_tech
		NOT = {
			has_modifier = gaudi_italo_balloon_modifier
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_no_italo_balloon
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_PIEDMONT
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_mole_state
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.424.g #A tourist balloon sounds like a good idea
		default_option = yes
		add_treasury = -7500
		gaudi_add_3_mole_progress = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_italo_balloon_modifier
			years = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gaudi.424.h #A tourist balloon sounds like a good idea
		gaudi_add_1_mole_progress = yes
		set_variable = gaudi_no_italo_balloon
	}
}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		any_scope_state = {
			has_modifier = gaudi_italo_balloon_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_PIEDMONT
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_mole_state

		}
	}

#Gaudí 501: Ringstrasse Phase 1 begins

	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.501.t
	desc = gaudi.501.d
	flavor = gaudi.501.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_ringstrasse_begin.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_AUSTRIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ringstrasse_state
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ruler
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.501.g
        default_option = yes
        scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state = {
        	add_modifier = {
        		name = gaudi_ringstrasse_phase_1_modifier
        	}
        }
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_ringstrasse_cost_1_modifier
		}
        add_journal_entry = {
        	type = je_gaudi_ringstrasse_phase_1
        }
	}
}

 				building = "building_gaudi_ringstrasse"
				level = 1

        }
		remove_modifier = gaudi_ringstrasse_cost_3_modifier
	}
}

#Gaudí 511: Fountain or Pavillon?

gaudi.511 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.511.t
	desc = gaudi.511.d
	flavor = gaudi.511.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_ringstrasse_fountain.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_ringstrasse_fountain_cooldown
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_AUSTRIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ringstrasse_state
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.511.g #We build the pavillon.
        default_option = yes
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
    			is_in_government = yes
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_supported_ringstrasse_project_modifier
				years = 2
			}
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
    			is_in_government = no
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_refused_ringstrasse_project_modifier
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.511.h #We build the fountain.
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
    			is_in_government = no
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_supported_ringstrasse_project_modifier
				years = 2
			}
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
    			is_in_government = yes
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_refused_ringstrasse_project_modifier
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.511.i #I have my own plans for this place...
		gaudi_add_6_ringstrasse_progress = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_vanity_project_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_refused_ringstrasse_project_modifier
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		set_variable = {
			name = gaudi_ringstrasse_fountain_cooldown
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

		scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state = {

				value = 0.05
				pop_type = officers
			}
		}
	}

		set_variable = {
			name = gaudi_ringstrasse_statues_cooldown
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 514: New Coffee house

	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.514.t
	desc = gaudi.514.d
	flavor = gaudi.514.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_ringstrasse_coffee.dds"
	}

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			any_scope_character = {
				is_ruler = yes
				has_modifier = gaudi_coffee_house_connoisseur_modifier
			}
			any_scope_state = {
				has_modifier = gaudi_coffeehouse_culture_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_AUSTRIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ringstrasse_state
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ruler
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.514.g #$MONARCH$ should visit it
        default_option = yes
		scope:gaudi_ruler = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_coffee_house_connoisseur_modifier
			}
		}
		gaudi_add_6_ringstrasse_progress = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.514.h #This will raise the standard of living in Vienna
        default_option = yes
		scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_coffeehouse_culture_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		gaudi_add_3_ringstrasse_progress = yes	
	}
}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_ringstrasse_ringpalais_cooldown
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_AUSTRIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ringstrasse_state
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ruler
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.515.g #We share the costs.
        default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_ringpalais_cost_modifier
			years = 3
		}
		gaudi_add_6_ringstrasse_progress = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.515.h #That's none of our business.
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_sub_9_ringstrasse_progress = yes	
	}

	after = {
		set_variable = {
			name = gaudi_ringstrasse_ringpalais_cooldown
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 520: Political Controversy

	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.520.t
	desc = gaudi.520.d
	flavor = gaudi.520.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:rural_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_ringstrasse_rural_ig_cooldown
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_AUSTRIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ringstrasse_state
		}
		ig:ig_rural_folk = {
			save_scope_as = rural_ig 
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = rural_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.520.g #How about a friendly gift for the benefit of the hard-working rural population?
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_sub_3_ringstrasse_progress = yes
		add_treasury = -10000
		scope:rural_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.520.h #City and province are equal.
		gaudi_sub_9_ringstrasse_progress = yes
		scope:rural_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.520.i #Who cares about this stupid farmer's talk?
		gaudi_sub_9_ringstrasse_progress = yes
		scope:rural_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_christo_ig_rebuked_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		set_variable = {
			name = gaudi_ringstrasse_rural_ig_cooldown
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 522: Extending the Barracks

gaudi.522 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.522.t
	desc = gaudi.522.d
	flavor = gaudi.522.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_ringstrasse_wall.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_AUSTRIA
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_barracks
				level <= 30
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_AUSTRIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ringstrasse_state
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.522.g #Expand the barracks.
		gaudi_sub_6_ringstrasse_progress = yes
		custom_tooltip = gaudi_add_barracks_tt
		scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state = {
			create_building = {
 				building = "building_barracks"
				level = 30
 			}
			activate_building = {
				building = "building_barracks"
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.522.h #Let's better invest the time elsewhere.
		default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_9_ringstrasse_progress = yes
	}
}

#Gaudí 527: Heldenplatz

gaudi.527 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.527.t
	desc = gaudi.527.d
	flavor = gaudi.527.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_ringstrasse_heldenplatz.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_ringstrasse_heldenplatz_var
		}
		global_var:gaudi_ringstrasse_progress >= 60
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_AUSTRIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ringstrasse_state
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = root
     				type = alliance 
     			}
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ally_nation
		}
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			save_scope_as = army_ig
		}
		set_variable = gaudi_ringstrasse_heldenplatz_var
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.527.g #Hold a parade and invite our friends.
		default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_3_ringstrasse_progress = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_heldenplatz_parade_friends_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:gaudi_ally_nation = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 10
			}
		}
		add_treasury = -10000
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.527.h #Establish a permanent military parade for the next few years.
		gaudi_add_1_ringstrasse_progress = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_heldenplatz_parade_military_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_heldenplatz_parade_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		add_treasury = -20000
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.527.i #And who should pay for all this?
		gaudi_add_6_ringstrasse_progress = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_heldenplatz_miser_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

		custom_tooltip = gaudi_add_hall_tt
		scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state = {
			create_building = {
 				building = "building_arts_academy"
				level = 10
 			}
			activate_building = {
				building = "building_arts_academy"
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.522.h #Let's better invest the time elsewhere.
		default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_9_ringstrasse_progress = yes
	}
}

#Gaudí 530: Urania

gaudi.530 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.530.t
	desc = gaudi.530.d
	flavor = gaudi.530.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_ringstrasse_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_ringstrasse_urania.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_ringstrasse_urania_var
		}
		global_var:gaudi_ringstrasse_progress >= 60
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_AUSTRIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ringstrasse_state
		}
		set_variable = gaudi_ringstrasse_urania_var
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.530.g #It is an architectural landmark.
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = elgar_art_nouveau_tech
		}
		custom_tooltip = gaudi.530.tt
		default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_1_splendid_architecture = yes
		gaudi_add_1_ringstrasse_progress = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.530.h #It is primarily an entertainment establishment.
		elgar_add_x_music_tradition_effect = { AMOUNT = 25 }
		gaudi_add_1_ringstrasse_progress = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.530.i #First and foremost this is an observatory.
		verrier_add_x_astronomical_objects_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 10
		}
		gaudi_add_1_ringstrasse_progress = yes
	}
}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_CATALONIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_sagrada_state
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}

		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.601.g
        default_option = yes
        scope:gaudi_sagrada_state = {
        	add_modifier = {
        		name = gaudi_sagrada_phase_1_modifier
        	}
        }
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_sagrada_cost_1_modifier

        	type = je_gaudi_sagrada_phase_1
        }
	}
}

		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = pious
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_sagrada_donator
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = gaudi.631.g #
		gaudi_add_3_sagrada_progress = yes
		scope:gaudi_sagrada_donator = {
			set_variable = gaudi_sagrada_pious_support
		}
	}

#Gaudi 632: Clergy happy

gaudi.632= {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.632.t
	desc = gaudi.632.d
	flavor = gaudi.632.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_sagrada_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:devout_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_sagrada_devout_support
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = gaudi_sagrada_devout_support
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_CATALONIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_sagrada_state
		}
		ig:ig_devout = {
			save_scope_as = devout_ig 
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = devout_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = gaudi.632.g #We should benefit from that
		gaudi_add_6_sagrada_progress = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_sagrada_devout_influence_modifier
			years = 5
		}

	}
	option = {
		name = gaudi.632.h #Praise the Church in public
        default_option = yes
		scope:devout_ig   = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gaudi.632.i # This matter does not involve the church!
		gaudi_sub_1_sagrada_progress = yes
        add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_sagrada_devout_rebuked_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 635: Atheistic intervention

	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.635.t
	desc = gaudi.635.d
	flavor = gaudi.635.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_sagrada_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_sagrada_atheist

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		any_scope_character = {
			has_ideology = ideology:ideology_atheist
			NOT = {
				has_variable = gaudi_sagrada_atheist
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_CATALONIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_sagrada_state
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_ideology = ideology:ideology_atheist
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_sagrada_atheist
			set_variable = gaudi_sagrada_atheist
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = gaudi.635.g #
		gaudi_sub_6_sagrada_progress = yes
		default_option = yes
	}
	option = { 
		name = gaudi.635.h #
		gaudi_add_3_sagrada_progress = yes
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				has_ideology = ideology:ideology_anti_clerical
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_sagrada_ig_rebuked_modifier
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 644: Romantic/pious ruler

gaudi.644 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.644.t
	desc = gaudi.644.d
	flavor = gaudi.644.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_sagrada_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_ruler

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_romantic_ruler_support
		}
		any_scope_character = {
			is_ruler = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = romantic
				has_trait = pious
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_CATALONIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_sagrada_state
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = romantic
					has_trait = pious
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ruler
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.644.g #Our good [title] [fullname]!
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_6_sagrada_progress = yes
		set_variable = {
			name = gaudi_romantic_ruler_support
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 645: Inviting an Ally

gaudi.645 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.645.t
	desc = gaudi.645.d
	flavor = gaudi.645.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_sagrada_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_sagrada_9.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		any_country = {
			has_diplomatic_pact = {
				who = root
     			type = alliance 
     		}
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = gaudi_sagrada_patron_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_CATALONIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_sagrada_state
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = root
     				type = alliance 
     			}
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ally_nation
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.645.g #Invite our ally to visit Cologne.
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_3_sagrada_progress = yes
		scope:gaudi_ally_nation = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 5
			}
		}
		scope:gaudi_ally_nation = {
			trigger_event = { 
				id = gaudi.646
				popup = yes 
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gaudi.645.h #This will only disturb our efforts.
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_1_sagrada_progress = yes
	}
}

#Gaudí 646: Donation to the cathedral?

gaudi.646 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.646.t
	desc = gaudi.646.d
	flavor = gaudi.646.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_sagrada_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_sagrada_9.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_CATALONIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_sagrada_state
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					state_region = s:STATE_CATALONIA
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_sagrada_nation
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.646.g #This splendid project should have our support.
        default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_sagrada_patron_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			days = 1000
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_diplomatic_prestige_modifier
			days = 1000
		}
		scope:gaudi_sagrada_nation = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 5
			}
		}
		scope:gaudi_sagrada_nation = {
			trigger_event = { 
				id = gaudi.647
				popup = yes 
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gaudi.646.h #It's not that great after all.
		scope:gaudi_sagrada_nation = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -5
			}
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 648: Archaeological investigations

gaudi.648 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.648.t
	desc = gaudi.648.d
	flavor = gaudi.648.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_sagrada_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_archaeologist

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_excavation_barcelona
		}
		lepsius_has_active_archaeologist = yes
		global_var:gaudi_sagrada_progress >= 12
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_CATALONIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_sagrada_state
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = gaudi_archaeologist
		}
		set_variable = gaudi_excavation_barcelona
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.648.g #We cannot afford such a long halt to construction.
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_1_sagrada_progress = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.648.h #A unique archaeological opportunity.
		gaudi_sub_12_sagrada_progress = yes
		lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = { 
			AMOUNT = 2
		}
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "10"
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.701.t
	desc = gaudi.701.d
	flavor = gaudi.701.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_neuschwanstein_state

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_neuschwanstein_begin.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BAVARIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_neuschwanstein_state
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ruler
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.701.g
        default_option = yes
        scope:gaudi_neuschwanstein_state = {
        	add_modifier = {
        		name = gaudi_neuschwanstein_phase_1_modifier
        	}
        }
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_neuschwanstein_cost_1_modifier
		}
        add_journal_entry = {
        	type = je_gaudi_neuschwanstein_phase_1
        }
	}
}

		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BAVARIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_neuschwanstein_state
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.111.g #If you want to do it well, it takes longer
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_x_neuschwanstein_progress = {
			AMOUNT = -1
		}
		add_treasury = -10000
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.111.h #That's okay.
		gaudi_add_x_neuschwanstein_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 3
		}
		add_treasury = 20000
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				35 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = gaudi.717
						days = { 14 21 }
					}
				}
				50 = { }
				15 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = gaudi.712
						days = { 14 21 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 713: Opposition criticizes Neuschwanstein

gaudi.713 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.713.t
	desc = gaudi.713.d
	flavor = gaudi.713.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_neuschwanstein_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_opposition_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = 3
	}

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BAVARIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_neuschwanstein_state
		}
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
    			is_in_government = no
	        }
			save_scope_as = gaudi_opposition_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = gaudi_opposition_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.713.g #I'm the King and I build what I want!
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_x_neuschwanstein_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 3
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_neuschwanstein_defender_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:gaudi_opposition_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 5
			}
		}
		scope:gaudi_neuschwanstein_state = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = 0.02
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.713.h #Maybe this IS vanity?
		gaudi_add_x_neuschwanstein_progress = {
			AMOUNT = -6
		}
		scope:gaudi_opposition_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 3
			}
		}
		scope:gaudi_neuschwanstein_state = {
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				value = 0.02
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_neuschwanstein_machines
		}
		any_scope_building = {
			is_building_type = building_motor_industry
		}
		has_technology_researched = steel_frame_buildings
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BAVARIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_neuschwanstein_state
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.124.g #This is progress!
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_x_neuschwanstein_progress = {
			"AMOUNT" = 12
		}
		set_variable = gaudi_neuschwanstein_machines
	}
}

#Gaudí 715: Neighbour impressed

gaudi.715 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.715.t
	desc = gaudi.715.d
	flavor = gaudi.715.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_neuschwanstein_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_neuschwanstein_bedroom.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = 5
	}

	trigger = {
		any_country = {
			has_diplomatic_pact = {
				who = root
     			type = alliance 
     		}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BAVARIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_neuschwanstein_state
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_adjacent_to_country = ROOT
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_neighbour_nation
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.715.g #Show the ambassador Neuschwanstein.
        default_option = yes
		change_infamy = -3
		scope:gaudi_neighbour_nation = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 10
			}
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:gaudi_neighbour_nation 
			value = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gaudi.715.h #Ask for a donation.
		add_treasury = 10000
		gaudi_add_x_neuschwanstein_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 3
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 718: A National or a Royal Project?

gaudi.718 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.718.t
	desc = gaudi.718.d
	flavor = gaudi.718.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_neuschwanstein_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:landowners_leader
	right_icon = scope:intelligentsia_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_neuschwanstein_royalism_nationalism_conflict_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = gaudi_neuschwanstein_royalism_nationalism_conflict_var
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BAVARIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_neuschwanstein_state
		}
		ig:ig_landowners = {
			save_scope_as = landowners_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = landowners_leader
			}
		}
		ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
			save_scope_as = intelligentsia_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = intelligentsia_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.718.g #This is a castle for the nation.
        gaudi_add_x_neuschwanstein_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 6
		}
		scope:intelligentsia_ig  = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
		scope:landowners_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.718.h #This is a national and a monarchist project
		gaudi_add_x_neuschwanstein_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 1
		}
		default_option = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.718.i #This is a castle for the king.
        gaudi_add_x_neuschwanstein_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 6
		}
		scope:intelligentsia_ig  = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
		scope:landowners_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

#Gaudí 721: "Verein der Handwerker am königlichen Schlossbau zu Hohenschwangau"

gaudi.721 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.721.t
	desc = gaudi.721.d
	flavor = gaudi.721.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_neuschwanstein_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_union_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = 100
	}

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BAVARIA
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_neuschwanstein_state
		}
		ig:ig_trade_unions = {
			save_scope_as = trade_unions_ig 
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = gaudi_union_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.721.g #An institution worth supporting
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_x_neuschwanstein_progress = {
			AMOUNT = -3
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_neuschwanstein_verein_modifier
			years = 10
		}
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 3
			}
		}
		scope:gaudi_neuschwanstein_state = {
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				value = 0.2
				pop_type = laborers
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.721.h #A role model for the whole country!
		add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_neuschwanstein_verein_modifier
			years = 10
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				law_stance = {
					law = law_type:law_wage_subsidies
					value > neutral
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = manzoni_political_tailwind_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 5
			}
		}
		scope:gaudi_neuschwanstein_state = {
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				value = 0.1
				pop_type = laborers
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.721.i #Social assistance? I need workers, not whiners!
		gaudi_add_x_neuschwanstein_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 6
		}
		scope:gaudi_neuschwanstein_state = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = 0.1
				pop_type = laborers
			}
		}
	}
}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {

			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_MEXICO
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_palacio_state

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_MEXICO
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_palacio_state
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_ruler
		}
		set_global_variable = gaudi_palacio_finished
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.804.g
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_2_splendid_architecture = yes
        scope:gaudi_palacio_state = {
        	remove_modifier = gaudi_palacio_phase_2_modifier
        }
		scope:gaudi_palacio_state = {
			create_building = {
 				building = "building_gaudi_palacio"
				level = 1
 			}
        }
		remove_modifier = gaudi_palacio_cost_2_modifier
	}
}

#Gaudí 812: Trade unions unhappy

gaudi.812 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.812.t
	desc = gaudi.812.d
	flavor = gaudi.812.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_palacio_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:trade_unions_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_modifier = gaudi_palacio_better_worker_conditions_modifier
		}
		ig:ig_trade_unions = {
			is_in_government = no
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_MEXICO
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_palacio_state
		}
		ig:ig_trade_unions = {
			save_scope_as = trade_unions_ig 
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = trade_unions_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = gaudi.633.g #Ignore them
		gaudi_add_x_palacio_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 1
		}
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 4
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gaudi.633.h #Pay lip service
        default_option = yes
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gaudi.633.i #Spend money to improve the worker's situation
		custom_tooltip = gaudi.314.tt
		gaudi_add_x_palacio_progress = {
			AMOUNT = -3
		}
        add_modifier = {
			name = gaudi_palacio_better_worker_conditions_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:trade_unions_ig  = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

gaudi.818 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.818.t
	desc = gaudi.818.d
	flavor = gaudi.818.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_palacio_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_archaeologist

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = gaudi_excavation_mexico
		}
		lepsius_has_active_archaeologist = yes
		global_var:gaudi_palacio_progress >= 12
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_MEXICO
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_palacio_state
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = gaudi_archaeologist
		}
		set_variable = gaudi_excavation_mexico
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.648.g #We cannot afford such a long halt to construction.
        default_option = yes
		gaudi_add_x_palacio_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.648.h #A unique archaeological opportunity.
		gaudi_add_x_palacio_progress = {
			AMOUNT = -12
		}
		lepsius_add_x_precolumbian_artifacts_effect = { 
			AMOUNT = 2
		}
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "10"
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Gaudí 1001: Invention of the Steel Frame (Eiffel)

gaudi.1001 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.1001.t

	desc = gaudi.1001.d

	flavor = gaudi.1001.f

	placement = ROOT

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_engineer_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_architecture.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = steel_frame_buildings
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = gaudi_steel_frame_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = gaudi_steel_frame_var
		if = {
			limit ={
				NOT = {
					has_variable = gaudi_engineer_var
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					c:FRA ?= this
					NOT = {
						has_global_variable = mr_eiffel_created_global_var
					}
				}
				create_eiffel_gustave_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				create_new_engineer_effect = yes
				gaudi_set_new_engineer_as_engineer_effect = yes
				var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
					save_scope_as = gaudi_engineer_scope
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
					NOT = { has_trait = gaudi_civil_engineer }
				}
			}
			var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
				add_trait = gaudi_civil_engineer
			}
		}
		var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
			set_variable = gaudi_engineer_invented_steel_frame_var
			save_scope_as = gaudi_engineer_scope
		}
		set_variable = gaudi_first_invented_steel_frame_var
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.1001.g #Our towers will finally reach the sky!
		default_option = yes
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Gaudí 1006: The first Automobile with an Internal Combustion Engine

gaudi.1006 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.1006.t
	desc = gaudi.1006.d
	flavor = gaudi.1006.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_car_state_1_scope

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_engineer_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/automobiles.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = combustion_engine
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = gaudi_first_car_global_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = gaudi_first_car_global_var
		random_scope_state = {
			save_scope_as = gaudi_car_state_1_scope
		}
		scope:gaudi_car_state_1_scope = {
			random_neighbouring_state = {
				save_scope_as = gaudi_car_state_2_scope
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit ={
				NOT = {
					has_variable = gaudi_engineer_var
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BADEN
					year > 1864
					NOT = {
						has_global_variable = mr_benz_created_global_var_global_var
					}
				}
				create_benz_carl_effect = yes
				gaudi_set_new_engineer_as_engineer_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				create_new_engineer_effect = yes
				gaudi_set_new_engineer_as_engineer_effect = yes
				var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
					save_scope_as = gaudi_engineer_scope
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
					NOT = { has_trait = gaudi_mechanical_engineer }
				}
			}
			var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
				add_trait = gaudi_mechanical_engineer
			}
		}
		var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
			set_variable = gaudi_engineer_invented_automobile_var
			set_variable = {
				name = gaudi_engineer_invented_automobile_year_var
				value = year
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_engineer_scope
		}
		set_variable = gaudi_first_car_global_var
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.1006.g #Vroom!
		default_option = yes
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Gaudí 1221: The Mechanical Computer

gaudi.1221 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.1221.t
	desc = gaudi.1221.d
	flavor = gaudi.1221.f

	event_image = {
		#Photo of Babbage Analytical Engine Plan from 1840 at the Computer History Museum
		# CC BY 4.0 by ArnoldReinhold
		# https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Analytical_engine#/media/File:Babbage_Analytical_Engine_Plan_1840_CHM.agr.jpg
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_analytical_engine.dds"
	}	

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/machinists.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			#The global variable saves the first country that first invents the mechanical computer.
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_variable = gaudi_mechanical_computer_inventor_global_var }
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = gaudi_mechanical_computer_inventor_global_var
				value = root.country_definition
			}
			#Used for enineer achievement loc
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = gaudi_engineer_var }
				var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
					set_variable = gaudi_mechanical_computer_project_finished_engineer_var
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.1221.g #A true Marvel of Enineering
		default_option = yes

		mechanical_engineer_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 25 }
	}
}

#Gaudí 1222: The Analytical Engine
gaudi.1222 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.1222.t
	desc = gaudi.1222.d
	flavor = gaudi.1222.f

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid
	left_icon = scope:gaudi_new_engineer_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/machinists.dds"

	trigger = {
		year >= 1836
		c:GBR ?= this
	}

	immediate = {
		create_babbage_charles_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.1222.g #What a fascinating Project!

		add_journal_entry = { type = je_gaudi_mechanical_computer_project }
		#Informing the player about the costs of the project (Is actually applied in the JE)
		show_as_tooltip = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_engineer_project_very_high_cost_modifier
			}
		}
		#This part is used to add already existing progress to the project.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = gaudi_mechanical_computer_progress_save_var
			}
			je:je_gaudi_mechanical_computer_project = {
				set_bar_progress = {
					value = owner.var:gaudi_mechanical_computer_progress_save_var
					name = gaudi_mechanical_computer_project_progress_bar
				}
			}
		}
		#Sets Babbage as the new engineer
		gaudi_set_new_engineer_as_engineer_effect = yes
		#Makes the Engineer busy
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = gaudi_engineer_var
			}
			var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
				set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.1222.h #We could build so many warships instead!
		default_option = yes

		gaudi_remove_new_engineer_effect = yes
	}
}

gaudi.1301 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.1301.t
	desc = gaudi.1301.d
	flavor = gaudi.1301.f

	event_image = { #Chassot
		trigger = {
			var:gaudi_military_engineer_advanced_weapon = 1
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_engineering_military_chassepot_rifle.dds"
	}
	event_image = { #M1918
	trigger = {
		var:gaudi_military_engineer_advanced_weapon = 2
	}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_engineering_military_m1918.dds"
	}
	event_image = { #Thompson M1928
	trigger = {
		var:gaudi_military_engineer_advanced_weapon > 2
	}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gaudi_pictures/gaudi_engineering_military_tommy.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_rifling.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = gaudi_military_engineer_advanced_weapon } }
			set_variable = {
				name = gaudi_military_engineer_advanced_weapon
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = {
				name = gaudi_military_engineer_advanced_weapon
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = gaudi_engineer_var }
			var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
				set_variable = gaudi_rifles_project_finished_engineer_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.1301.g #A fascinating weapon. I should try it out immediately!
		default_option = yes

		custom_tooltip = gaudi_new_rifle_mobilization_option_tt
		gaudi_military_engineering_medium_add_technology = yes
		military_engineer_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 25 }
	}
	after = {
	}
}

######GEOMAGNETISM######

#Gaudí 1401: Admission to the Göttingen Magnetic Association

gaudi.1401 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.1401.t
	desc = gaudi.1401.d
	flavor = gaudi.1401.f

	placement = scope:gaudi_association_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_engineer_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/electrical_generation.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
			save_scope_as = gaudi_engineer_scope
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_HANNOVER
			}
			save_scope_as = gaudi_association_state
			owner = {
				save_scope_as = gaudi_goettingen_owner
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.1401.g #We should build a measuring station immediately.
		default_option = yes
		scope:gaudi_engineer_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		electrical_engineer_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 15 }
		gaudi_add_magnetic_association_member = yes
		gaudi_electrical_engineering_small_add_technology = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = gaudi_magnetic_association_member_var
				NOT = {
					ROOT = THIS
				}
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT
				value = 2
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Gaudí 1402: First records of the earth's magnetic field in $COUNTRY$

gaudi.1402 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.1402.t
	desc = gaudi.1402.d
	flavor = gaudi.1402.f

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_engineer_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/electrical_generation.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
			save_scope_as = gaudi_engineer_scope
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_HANNOVER
			}
			owner = {
				save_scope_as = gaudi_goettingen_owner
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = gaudi_engineer_var }
			var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
				set_variable = gaudi_geomagnetic_observartory_project_finished_engineer_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

			AMOUNT = 5
		}

			limit = {
				has_building = building_verrier_observatory
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_verrier_observatory
				production_method = pm_gaudi_magnetic_observatory
			}
		}
	}

	after = {

#Gaudí 1411: A National Telegraphy Network

gaudi.1411 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = gaudi.1411.t
	desc = gaudi.1411.d
	flavor = gaudi.1411.f

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_engineer_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_telegraph.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
			save_scope_as = gaudi_engineer_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gaudi.1411.g #The expansion of telegraphy has the highest priority.
		default_option = yes
		scope:gaudi_engineer_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_scope_state = {
						is_capital = yes
						any_scope_building = {
							is_building_type = building_railway
							has_active_production_method = pm_gaudi_telegraph_office
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				activate_production_method = {
					building_type = building_railway
					production_method = pm_gaudi_telegraph_office
				}
			}
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_gaudi_telegraphy_network
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}
